<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:joekel.html>joekel</a> (18986)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Romani language">Romani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="rom">ʒukel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dog</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">جاهل</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jâhel</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foolish, ignorant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">جاهِل</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jāhil</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ignorant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense development from <i>dog</i> to <i>large entity</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> mediated by the sense <i>large dog</i>.
</p>

***joey.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:joey.html>joey</a> (2027)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown. Older and more general sources state that <i><a href = vnd.unilang:joey.html>joey</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> from an Australian aboriginal language, but newer sources that focus on Australian English and aboriginal languages say the origin <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unknown. <i>The Australian National Dictionary</i> includes a sense of “young possum” with citations predating the earliest “young kangaroo” citations.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:joey.html>joey</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:joeys.html>joeys</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The immature young of a marsupial, notably a <a href = vnd.unilang:junior.html>junior</a> kangaroo, but also a young wallaby, koala, etc.</li>
<li>The shorter word whose <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a> can be found within a kangaroo word.
<ul><li><b>1998</b>, Richard Lederer, <a href = vnd.unilang:dave.html>Dave</a> Morice, <i>The Word <a href = vnd.unilang:circus.html>Circus</a></i> (page 129)
<dl><dd>Among the kangaroo <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> that yield the most joviality and joy are those that conceal multiple <b><a href = vnd.unilang:joeys.html>joeys</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2005</b>, Anu Garg, <i>Another Word a Day</i> (page 132)
<dl><dd>Sometimes a kangaroo word <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> more than one <b><a href = vnd.unilang:joey.html>joey</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> prison  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A parcel smuggled in to an inmate.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b>,  John Hoskison,  <cite>Inside: One <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a>'s Experience of Prison</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"Visit in two days though," <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> Tommo. "Hang in there <a href = vnd.unilang:mate.html>mate</a>, got a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:joey.html>joey</a></b> coming, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> be sweet then."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Grimaldi" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joseph Grimaldi">Joseph Grimaldi</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:joey.html>joey</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:joeys.html>joeys</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:circus.html>circus</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:clown.html>clown</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:joey.html>joey</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:joeys.html>joeys</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A member of the Royal Marines.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">jolly</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joey_Deacon" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joey Deacon"><a href = vnd.unilang:joey.html>Joey</a> Deacon</a>, who <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the focus of <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blue_Peter" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Blue Peter">Blue <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a></a>'</i>s 1981 charity campaign. The programme <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> aimed at children, who then picked the term up and used it as an insult.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:joey.html>joey</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:joeys.html>joeys</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive  in  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person with cerebal palsy.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive  in  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A stupid person.</li></ol>

***jong.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jong.html>jong</a> (859)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">jonc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">jung</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*jung</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jungaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂yuh₁n̥ḱós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jong.html>jong</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jonger.html>jonger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">jongst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>young</li>
<li>new</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jong.html>jong</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jongen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jonkie.html>jonkie</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">jongske</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jong.html>jong</a></strong>

***jongeling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jongeling.html>jongeling</a> (25758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Diachronically from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">jongelinc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">iungelig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jungilingaz</i>. Synchronically <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jong.html>jong</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ling</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***jongen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jongen</a> (264)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:jonge.html>jonge</a></i>, the <i>-n</i> derived from declined forms. Equivalent to nominal use of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jong.html>jong</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">young</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Junge</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jongen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jongens.html>jongens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jongetje.html>jongetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A boy, any male child.
<ul><li><b>1915</b>, Nescio (pseudonum of Jan Hendrik Frederik Grönloh), <i>Titaantjes</i>, page 1.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:jongens.html>Jongens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardige.html>aardige</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jongens.html>jongens</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>Al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeg.html>zeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelf.html>zelf</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Boys</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> — but <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> nice <b>boys</b>. If I say so myself.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> Members of a male 'peers' group, e.g. a military unit.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> used in the plural<span class="ib-comma">,</span> used in the vocative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Informal term used to address multiple children of masculine or mixed gender;</span> kids, guys <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">may be considered insufficiently gender-inclusive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> used in the vocative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Colloquial term used by <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> to address other familiar <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a></span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:mate.html>mate</a>, dude, <a href = vnd.unilang:bro.html>bro</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">familiar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A male servant, especially but not exclusively a younger one <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">using it for older <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> may be dated and offensive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">familiar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A male trainee or newcomer in a job.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The diminutive loses the <i>-n</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jonker.html>jonker</a> (64528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">joncker</i>. Equivalent to a corruption of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jonkheer.html>jonkheer</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A young male noble, often lacking a knighthood or a noble title of his own.</li>
<li>An untitled nobleman; <a href = vnd.unilang:baron.html>baron</a>, squire.</li>

***jota.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jota.html>jota</a> (60494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἰῶτα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iôta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense "small amount" developed in reference to a phrase in the New <a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>Testament</a>: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:eer.html>Eer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hemel.html>hemel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergaat.html>vergaat</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> één <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jota.html>jota</a></b> of één tittel <a href = vnd.unilang:vergaan.html>vergaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a>.</i>— <i>until heaven and earth pass away, not an iota, not a dot, will pass from the Law</i> (Mt 5:18), iota being the smallest letter of the Greek alphabet.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jota.html>jota</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jota.html>jota</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jota.html>jotaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">iota</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">Greek letter</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polarity_item" class="extiw" title="w:Polarity item">negative polarity item</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">iota</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">small amount</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:snap.html>snap</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jota.html>jota</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I don’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> understand a thing of it.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*jū</i>, a northern (Frisian?) variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*iu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*iwwiz</i>, a West Germanic variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*izwiz</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i>.

</p>

</p>
<ol><li>a logbook of a ship

<li>a notebook for accounting</li></ol>

***joviaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:joviaal.html>joviaal</a> (82360)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">jovial</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">gioviale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ioviālis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:joviaal.html>joviaal</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:joviaal.html>jovialer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">joviaalst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>jovial, merry, cheerful</li>
<li>good-humored, friendly, <a href = vnd.unilang:relaxed.html>relaxed</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">deva</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">jovialiteit</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">Jupiter</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeus.html>Zeus</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">juffrouwe</i>, an alternative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">joncfrouwe</i> (from where <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jonkvrouw.html>jonkvrouw</a></i>).

***juist.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juist</a> (419)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">juust</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">juste</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">iūstus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Italic language">Proto-Italic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="itc-pro">*jowestos</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂yew-</i>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">just</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juist</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juister</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juist</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">juistst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>right, correct
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">correct</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onjuist.html>onjuist</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:foutief.html>foutief</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>just</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juist</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>just, at that <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juist</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeluk.html>ongeluk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebeuren.html>gebeuren</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>just</b> coming back from work, when I saw an accident happen.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<li>exactly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>Zo</a>’n <a href = vnd.unilang:laffe.html>laffe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitvlucht.html>uitvlucht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juist</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Such a lame excuse from your part <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>exactly</b> what I didn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> want to hear.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
